<rating>5< /rating><review>Great happy hour special! Everyday from 12 - 3 pm and 5 - 7 pm. 1 roll and 5 pieces of sushi with miso soup and edamame for just $9.99. There are plenty of rolls to choose from so I'm sure you will find the perfect one. Plus 50% off beers and sake. My favorite has to be the Double Double. It comes with avocado and salmon on the inside AND avocado and salmon on the outside. Just thinking about it makes my mouth water. Just as the name suggest, I loved the Ai roll. They love to take advantage of being a Denti-Cal provider. If you're on Denti-Cal, they will view you as a money bag. They took x-rays even when they weren't needed, as I had some I could've sent them from my last dentist. They had me show up for surgery one day just to tell me that my tooth was too close to the nerve, so they needed to file for sedation approval with Denti-Cal. Appointment fee they just exploited from Denti-Cal right there.This is a conclusion even Patrick Star could've come to just by looking at the x-ray. When I finally did go for my wisdom teeth removal surgery 5 months later after first seeing them, it was one of the worst days of my life. they gave me two days notice to find. a driver who could stay on the premises during my surgery, and when I wet in and tried to explain to them I could make that happen, the receptionist says no you need a driver or this isn't happening today. I tell her we are in a effing pandemic and you guys only gave me two days notice to find a driver who could STAY. Her attitude falls to the floor, and then has the audacity to say "It's always something with you every time you come here, isn't it?" I respond by saying well maybe it's because your customer service as a business is sub-prime and there's always a reason to complain about something at this god-foresaken place. She hands me forms to sign, and says that they won't do it unless the driver stays. My driver says its fine, he can stay in his car and use his wifi hotspot, since the clinic refused to offer him wifi to do his work with. There was no reason for them to schedule me at 8 in the morning for 5 minutes of paperwork when they actually didn't open till NINE. So stupid. After I woke up, apparently I was crying and screaming. This was when the staff showed their true colors. All Western Dental sees its customers as is a money bag. They lack any basic customer service skills. When I couldn't stop crying, they forced me into a wheelchair and shoved me into my roommates car. I will never go back to this place. Don't waste your time, your money, or your mental sanity on this place. Ever.</review>

My dentist was nice but she seemed like she was either scatterbrained or didn't know what she was doing. I asked her multiple times if she could tell me how many cavities I had she always said give her a second I had to have asked at least 3 times and still have no idea how many I have I just know there are multiple but I could've figured that out from opening my mouth..

ALL THE DOWNSIDES: The receptionists are a different matter however. They are incredibly pushy with things your insurance wont cover so much so that you just want to say yes to make them stop talking. I heard the dental hygienist say she's having a hard time getting people to pick up a product she suggests (same one that I was pushed into) that the insurance doesn't cover and Im willing to bet that its the same reason as me we didn't want it but we wanted the receptionists to stop pushing.

The receptionists on top of that are rude, when I got my wisdom teeth pulled the lady acted like I was the worst human being on this planet for drinking water an hour earlier so I wouldn't be dehydrated and because I was only told not to eat food no one said anything about not drinking until it was time for my appointment.

The receptionists call multiple times to confirm appointments yet my appointment was canceled because the doctor had an emergency which is fine but she wouldn't be back until August 8 almost a month after my appointment was scheduled for and Im moving out of town they wanted me to reschedule for the 8th, um no. Thats a pain for me to have to come back after Ive moved when there are dentists all over the world. I asked if it was at all possible to get something this month explained I'm moving and really want to get it out of the way keep in mind I talked to three people about this. One on the phone, two at the receptionists desk and they acted like I was the rudest person for coming in to talk face to face, I work two blocks away and my apartment is in that direction its literally on the way home for me like is it that hard to talk to someone in person? All of them took my information and said they have to talk to the manager to get approval for me to change doctors... Its been well over a week since I spoke to the two receptionist and 3 days before that I spoke to the receptionist on the phone.

I don't know if its bad management or the receptionists are just rude in general but I feel completely disrespected. There was literally no work done on my teeth aside from the wisdom teeth. This appointment was for fillings and I was supposed to make one for a root canal and yet I have yet to receive a call over a week later either from the manager or a receptionist. I wanted this all done before I moved and now I have to start all over again because apparently they cant even call someone back. They got my money and now their done with me is how it looks to be completely honest since even though I was told sedation for my wisdom teeth removal was a necessity I was also told my insurance wouldn't cover it.

< review>
Pleasantly suprised by their act of generosity. I came to Western Dental to obtain dental X-rays for my medical clearance into the Peace Corps. The copy I recieved turned out to be incomplete and I came back to address this issue, twice. Due to medical insurance policies, I was responsible for any additional costs. I do not know why the x-ray series was incopmplete to begin with. But, after I explained my situation, the receptionist assisting me (who was very cordial on both occasions) informed me that her manager had agreed to complete my dental x-rays at no cost. These were done by Chito, who behaved professionally. And, although I have experienced some of the complaints mentioned above- such as a long wait time- I am very pleased that the staff at Western Dental was able to help me on something that is very, personally, important.
Thank you.<//review>
